 dilli main ek baar phir adhikaron kii jang chhid gai he

 Bihar is in the grip of flood once again
 rajya kii 25 lakh se zyada kii aabaadi prabhavit he
 546 panchayats of 77 blocks of about 12 districts of the state are submerged in water
 ab tak 34 logon kii maut ho chuki he
 Despite the government's claims on this problem that has been going on for years, the situation is the same as it is every year
 pichley 40 saalon se yani 1979 se ab tak bihar lagaataar har saal baadh se jujh rahaa he
 According to the Bihar government's water resources department, 68,800 sq km of the state is submerged every year by floods
 aaie jaanate hai ki bihar har saal baadh main kyon dub jaataa he
 
 
 There are four major causes of floods in Bihar
 
 
 1
 Nepal releases water, so many areas of Bihar are submerged due to heavy rains in the border area of nepal and Bihar for the last two weeks, the water level of the rivers has increased drastically
 uttar bihar ke arriya, kishanganj, farbishganj, purniya, supaul, madhubani, darbhanga or katihaar jile main baadh kaa pani ghus gaya he
 Hundreds of villages along the banks of all the small and big rivers of North Bihar including Kosi, Kamla, Bagmati, Gandak, Mahananda have been submerged
 nepal main jab bhi pani kaa str badhata he vah apane baandhon ke daravaaje khol detaa he
 This causes floods in the districts of Bihar adjacent to Nepal
 2
 Farakka Barrage comes due to flooding After the formation of Farakka Barrage, river erosion has increased in Bihar
 sahaayak nadiyon dwaara laai gai gaad or ganga main ghatata jalpravaah samasya ko gambhir banaate hai
 Kosi, Gandak and Ghaghra, the tributaries of the Ganges coming from the Himalayas in Bihar, bring a lot of silt
 ise ve ganga main apane muhane par jamaa karti hai
 Because of this, water starts spreading to the surrounding areas
 nadi main gaad na ho or jalpravaah bana rahe to aisi samasya aae hi nahin
 3
 jarurat ke hisaab se tatbandhon kaa kam hona1954 main bihar main 160 kimi tatbandh tha
 Then 25 lakh hectares of land was flooded
 abhi kareeb 3700 kimi tatbandh hai lekin baadh se prabhavit kshetra badhkar 68
 90 lakh hectares
 jis tareeke se baadh main ijapha ho rahaa he, us hisaab se tatbandhon kii sankhya main badhotaree nahin ho rahi he
 4
 jalgrahan kshetron main pedo kii andhadhundh katibihar main jalgrahan kshetra (cachament aria) main pedo kii lagaataar andhadhundh kataai ho rahi he
 Because of this, water does not stop in the catchment area
 kosi nadi kaa cachament aria 74,030 varg kimi he
 Of this, 62,620 sq km is in Nepal and Tibet
 sirf 11,410 varg kimi hissaa hi bihar main he
 Nepal and Tibet, located on the mountains, receive more rainfall, then the water flows from the catchment area to the lower catchment area in Bihar
 pedo ke nahin hone kii vajah se pani cachament aria main na rukkar aabaadi vaale kshetron main fail jaataa he
 How much damage has been done since 1979? Bihar floods have resulted in 8570 deaths due to various reasons related to the floods
 25,776 maveshi or jaanavar maare gaye
 7
 70 karod hectare jameen baadh ke pani main dub gai
 3
 74 karod hectare jameen par lagi fasal kharaab ho gai
 7969 crore rupees have been lost due to crop failure
 1
 15 crore houses have been damaged
 4151 karod rupye kaa nuksaan hua he saarvajanik imaaraton ke tuutane se

 23 lakh se zyada log prabhavit
 More than 250 people died
 2013:july main ai baadh se 200 log maare gaye
 The impact of the flood was in 20 districts
 kareeb 50 lakh logon ke prabhavit hue
 2011: The impact of the flood was in 25 districts
 71
 The lives of 43 lakh people were affected
 249 logon kii jaan gai
 2008: 18 districts hit by floods
 50 lakh log prabhavit hue
 258 people died
 34 karod kii fasalein kharaab hui
 2007: Flood havoc in 22 districts
 1287 logon kii jaan chali gai
 2
 4 karod log prabhavit hue
 The United Nations called it the worst flood in the history of Bihar
 2004:20 jilon ke 9,346 gaanvon ke 2 karod se zyada log prabhavit hue
 885 people died
 522 karod kii fasalon kaa nuksaan hua
 2002: The impact of the flood was in 25 districts
 489 logon kii maut hui
 Crops worth more than 511 crore were destroyed
 8,318 gaanv jalmagn rahe
 2000: Flood effect in 33 districts
 12 hajaar se adhik gaanv baadh kii chapet main rahe
 336 people lost their lives

 1987 main ai baadh main 30 jilon ke 24518 gaanv prabhavit hue the

 The third T20 match played between India and England in Bengaluru was in the name of Haryana's young leg-spinner Yajuvendra Chahal despite the dominance of Suresh Raina, MS Dhoni, Yuvraj Singh, Eoin Morgan and Joe Root
 aise samay jab lag rahaa tha ki match romaanch kii oonchaaiyon ko chhu saktaa he or england kii batting team india ko barabari kii takkar detii najar aa rahi thi, chahal ek jhonke kii tarah aae or match par chaa gaye
 He took the third best performance of T20 by taking six wickets for 25 runs in the match
 swaabhaavik rup se 26 varshiya chahal hi main of da match or player of da siries ghoshit kiye gaye
 The comments match main jab team india ne suresh raina, emes dhoni or yuvaraj singh kii dhamaakedaar ballebaaji kii badaulat 202 kaa bada score khadaa kiya to bhartiya phens jeet ko lekar kaaphi had tak aashwast ho chuke the
 Playing in reply, when England lost two wickets on the score of 55 runs, then this victory seemed certain
 england kaa pehla wicket 8 ke score par or doosraa 55 ran ke score par gira
 By this time, the morale of the Indian team had reached the seventh sky
 iske baad shuru hui england ke captain eon morgan or jo root kii saajhedaari, jisane bhartiya gendbaajon ke khilaaf akraman kii niti akhriyaar karte hue na keval bhartiya team ko agali safalataa se vanchit rakhaa balki acchhee ran gati se score kaa raftaar di
 During this, Morgan scored 40 off 21 balls and Root scored 42 runs off 37 balls
 13 over ke baad england kaa score tha do wicket par 117 ran (ran ausat 9
 00), this time the visiting team needed 86 runs from 42 balls to win, which was very difficult in terms of T20 character but not impossible
 match photo finnish kii ore badhata najar aa rahaa tha
 In these moments, Chahal's third and 14th over innings changed the picture
 chahal ne iske baad lagaataar do gendon par morgan or root ko out kar patjhad kaa jo silsilaa shuru kiya vah aakhirkaar 127 par puri team ke out hone ke baad hi thama
 England's third and fourth wickets fell at the score of 119
 iske baad to ballebaajon main maano shunya par pavilion lautne kii hode much gai
 The sixth wicket was dismissed for 123 runs
 iske baad 127 ran par to england ne saatvaan, aathvaan, nauvaan or antim wicket ganvaa diya
 England's five batsmen were out on Billings, Butler, Plunkett, Jordan and Mils 0 while Adil Rashid remained unbeaten on the same score
 team india ne shandaar andaaj main aakhri tii20 match jitate hue test, vanade or tii20, tino formet main england kaa safaya kar diya
 In the match, when Team India scored a big score of 202 thanks to the explosive batting of Suresh Raina, MS Dhoni and Yuvraj Singh, the Indian fans were quite confident about the victory
 jawaab main khelte hue jab england ne 55 ran ke score par do wicket ganvaa die to yah jeet tay hi lagane lagi thi
 England's first wicket fell to a score of 8 and the second to a score of 55 runs
 is samay tak bhartiya team kaa manobal saatven aasmaan par pahunch chukaa tha
 It was followed by a partnership between England captain Eoin Morgan and Joe Root, who not only denied the Indian team any further success, but also scored at a good run rate, taking the attack policy against the Indian bowlers
 is dauraan morgan ne 21 gendon par 40 or root ne 37 gendon par 42 ran kii pari khel daali
 England's score after 13 overs was 117 runs for two wickets (9 runs scored)
 00), is samay mehmaan team ko jeet ke liye 42 gendon par 86 ran kii darkaar thi jo tii20 ke charitra ke lihaaj se behad mushkil jarur tha lekin asambhav nahin
 The match looked to be moving towards the photo finish
 in kshanon main chahal kaa teesraa or pari kaa 14waan over match kii tasviir badal gaya
 Chahal then started the procession of the fall by dismissing Morgan and Root for two consecutive balls, which finally came to an end after the entire team was dismissed at 127
 119 ke score par england kaa teesraa or chauthaa wicket gira
 After this, there was a competition among the batsmen to return to the pavilion at zero
 chatha wicket 123 ran par out hua
 After this, England lost the seventh, eighth, ninth and final wickets for 127 runs
 england ke paanch ballebaaj billings, butler, plunket, jordan or mills 0 par out hue jabaki adil raashid isi score par naabad rahe
 Team India defeated England in Test, ODI and T20, all three formats, winning the last T20 match in a spectacular manner
 match photo finnish kii ore badhata najar aa rahaa tha

 saamana main chape lekh ke mukhya ansh-janata ne bijepi kaa kachra kar diyajis loksabhaa chunaav main modi ke netritv main bhartiya janata party ko shat pratishat vijay hasil hui, usee dilli kii janata ne aap ke arvind kejariwal kii jhaadu haath main lekar bijepi kaa kachra kar diya, yah durbhagyavash kahana pad rahaa he
 The election in Delhi proved how fickle politics is
 vaade nahin kiye puure isliye janata ne nakarapradhanmantri narendra modi kaa nivas ab dilli main hi hua karata he, parantu itane nikat hokar bhi is baar modi kaa brahmastra nahin chalaa
 Amit Shah's magic did not work in the election
 dilli kaa chunaav parinaam tamaam arthon main, tamaam logon kaa parinaam he
 The Bharatiya Janata Party is our old cooperative friend
 sampurna desh main unhone loksabhaa or vidhansabha chunaav main padaakrant kiya, par desh kii rajdhani main unka camel nahin khil sakaa

 booth pramukhon kaa prabandhan, jaateey sameekaran or samgr satta ko jhonk dene se bhi manachaahe parinaam nahin hasil kiye ja sakate

 is nimitt bhartiya janata party main vyaapt asantosh or bechaini bhi prakat hui

 yah pehla sabak or matadaataaon ko koi apni nijee jaagir nahin maan saktaa yah doosraa sabak chunaav ne diya he

 maharashtra ke baad tsunami kaa pani aaj dilli ja pahunchaa

 bijepi ke logon ko lagata he ki yah paraabhav pradhanmantri narendra modi kaa nahin he

 duusare netaaon ke liye vahaan koi mauka nahin tha

 hamaara bhi vahi mat he

 modi samet bijepi ke tamaam bade netaaon ne kejariwal or rahul gandhi kaa apane bhaashanon main majaak udaaya

 railway recruitment board (railway Recruitment Board, RRB) ne group si eelpi, technitian pariksha kaa rigelt (RRB Result 2018) jari kar diya he

 pehle stage kii sibiti ke rigelt kaa logon ko lambey samay se intjaar tha

 pehle stage kii pariksha main paas hone vaale ummidavaaron ko duusare stage kii pariksha dene kaa mauka milegaa

 duusare stage kii sibiti kii pariksha centre or shift detail se judi jaankaree exam se 10 din pehle jari kar di jaaegi

 in) Fitch ratings have reduced Punjab National Bank's (PNB) viability rating from 'BB' to 'bbminus' after the bank's trillion rupee fraud and maintained Rating Watch at negative (RWN)
 credit reating agency dwaara jari ek bayaan ke mutabik, is downgrad se bank kii anya reating aprabhavit rahengi
 The statement said, "the downgrade assesses whether the financial mess that was busted in February of 2018 will affect the bank's financial position, its earnings and core capitalization
 yah downgrad bank ke jokhim niyantran ko darshata he, jiske bare main hamaara maananaa he ki pehle jitna bharosa tha, usase yah kamjor hua he
 Because the fraud had not been visible for many years and on a large scale2
 2 arab dollar kaa ghotaalaa kiya gaya tha
 The bank has said that it plans to strengthen its risk control
